## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Grafana Legacy Alerting to Unified Alerting Migration

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in grafana/grafana that implement both the legacy alerting engine and the unified alerting (ngalert) engine: the legacy alert rule storage, the unified alert rule storage, and the migration script that converts legacy rules to unified format.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec.


## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

The answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Key Files Found

### Legacy Alert Rule Storage
- **`pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/alert_mig.go`** — Creates the legacy `alert` table (and related tables: `alert_rule_tag`, `alert_notification`, `alert_notification_state`) that backed the old dashboard-linked alerting engine. The legacy runtime engine itself was removed in Grafana 11.

### Unified Alerting (ngalert) Engine
- **`pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go`** — The `AlertNG` service (unified alerting engine with scheduler, state manager, alertmanager)
- **`pkg/services/ngalert/store/database.go`** — `DBstore` struct and `AlertingStore` interface (unified alert storage layer)
- **`pkg/services/ngalert/store/alert_rule.go`** — CRUD operations for unified alert rules
- **`pkg/services/ngalert/models/alert_rule.go`** — `AlertRule` model with migration label constants like `MigratedLabelPrefix = "__legacy_"`

### Migration Script (Legacy → Unified)
- **`pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/ualert.go`** — Primary migration ("move dashboard alerts to unified alerting"), contains `upgradeNgAlerting` and `MigrationError`
- **`pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/tables.go`** — Creates unified alerting tables (`alert_rule`, `alert_instance`, etc.)
- **`pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/migration_service_migration.go`** — Moves migration status to kvstore
- **`pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/org_upgrade_state_mig.go`** — Per-org migration state tracking (`Legacy` vs `UnifiedAlerting`)
- **`pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/created_folders_mig.go`** — Migrates folder records created during legacy migration
- **`pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/migrations.go`** — Top-level migration orchestrator

            "content": "20: \n21: ## Scheduling and evaluation of alert rules\n22: \n23: The scheduling of alert rules happens in the `schedule` package. This package is responsible for managing the evaluation\n24: of alert rules including checking for new alert rules and stopping the evaluation of deleted alert rules.\n25: \n26: The scheduler runs at a fixed interval, called its heartbeat, in which it does a number of tasks:\n27: \n28: 1. Fetch the alert rules for all organizations (excluding disabled)\n29: 2. Start a goroutine (if this is a new alert rule or the scheduler has just started) to evaluate the alert rule\n30: 3.
